                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="880">
                       <div data-reactid="881">
                        <div data-reactid="882">
                         30 acres of: great views, serenity, hiking/horse trails, and off the grid mountaintop living. Was a Civil War encampment with fortifications used in the "Battle of Resaca". Has PRIVACY with a MOUNTAIN TOP location. Stay in the coziness of a VINTAGE AIRSTREAM. Refurbished with wood floors, original wood cabinets, kitchen, all in perfect condition. On a gated private road with no other people but the owners down the hill who seldom travel on the road. HORSES CAN BE STABLED FOR RIDING TRAILS.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="883">
                         The Airstream, of course, has every amenity you need for "off grid" living. Cooking is on a propane stove. A full size refrigerator with ample freezer and cool storage for a family's groceries. Hot water is ample for a cleansing shower after a day of hiking or just relaxing outside in the shade. Peace and quiet is only limited to the noise you make. Outside is a firepit with ample firewood for your use. Sit at the picnic table or pull up one of the lawn chairs to add to your outdoor pleasure. We are proud of our rural setting and it's natural beauty. Enjoy it by relaxing in or out of the trailer, hiking, riding your horse, or going to one of the nearby towns. PLEASE NOTE: Water is limited to what is in your tank. "Electricity" is 12V and battery powered. Yes, you are "glamping". There is a generator to provide AC in the summer on a limited basis and to charge the batteries during the day. At other times, the batteries provide ample power; but as with everything, there are limits.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="884">
                         We are definitely rural. The closest grocery store is 18 or so miles away. Yes, there are a few convenience stores closer. Major hospitals are within 20 to 30 minutes. We are heavily forested and fires can be a major hazard. Bicycling is a major recreational pastime on our curvy roads. Be careful. Our neighbors are mainly agricultural. Their land is pretty much private; but there are miles and miles of national forest for your pleasure just to the west and north. Civil War reenactments are held in the spring and you need to look up "Battle of Resaca", Tunnel Hill, and Chickamagua to name just a few. Hiking is all around. Keown Falls, The Pocket, John's Mountain, Chestnut Mountain, Dry Creek, and many more trails. Check out: (URL HIDDEN)
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="885">
                         <li data-reactid="886"><p data-reactid="887">The perfect getaway! The accommodations are immaculate (and I am a certified clean freak and Professional Organizer), the location is rustic and seems remote, but really is only 75 min from Atlanta. The Airstream and grounds are truly glamorous camping...more on the glamorous side as the hosts make sure you have everything, from a toaster, microwave oven to lounge chairs and a lantern for out by the fire! There is plenty of hiking, birdwatching, and views to make you forget the city rat race.                       <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1012">
                       <div data-reactid="1013">
                        <div data-reactid="1014">
                         Indoor camping! Adventurous people only! Sleeps 7. Coffee pot, microwave, mini fridge. Popular with rock climbers. It's part of our autoshop where cars are worked on. Lots of garage smells. Bathroom is across the cold and cluttered garage. Bring your friends and your pets! Professional pet sitter available.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1015">
                         Two adjoined rooms with one queen, two loft beds made from recycled pallets and a large sectional sofa. Wifi. No TV. Mini fridge, microwave, coffee pot. This school has been through desegregation, two families, a dog rescue, a commune, rental units and now is a forming intentional community. We have some rescue dogs, and barn cats. People have said it feels more like a large guest house. This is an older place, originally built in 1952. Expect all the smells of an older place. Being that it is attached to an autoshop, expect to smell oil. We have ten acres, 5 of which are fenced in. Feel free to wander the grounds, pet the animals , play in the auditorium, or sit outside to watch the ISS fly by or watch the chimney swifts come out right before sunset. Hang out and enjoy the way time slows down, or hop in your car and get to awesome rock climbing locations within the hour.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1016">
                         Our space is safe and secure. We live just 20 minutes from Chattanooga out in the country with easy and fast access to Chattanooga, hiking, rock climbing, kayaking, Lookout Mountain, and hang gliding. Chattanooga was voted America's best city 2015!! We are on the Iron Man Bike route. We are 5 miles from the Chickamauga Battlefield and 3.3 miles from Lee Gordon Mill and the Chickamauga Blue Way!
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="1017">
                         <li data-reactid="1018"><p data-reactid="1019">Amy and everyone at the school was fantastic! There were plenty of stories to hear and tell. We met more dogs then names I can remember, a few cats, some chicks, and the horse. The dogs and cats were very friendly, the horse only wants something to do with you if you've got apples! haha The bed was quite possibly the comfiest bed ever. The room was fantastic for the price, more then expected at such a low cost actually! The ceiling light went out on us once but came back on so no big deal (it's florescent lighting and as someone who works in an office I'm used to them flickering every now and then... besides, there is also a floor lamp that works just fine too). Everything else worked well (and yes, despite a previous review - there is hot water!). We were there visiting my grandmother in Chatsworth so we did not get a ton of one-on-one time with the hosts but enough to know they're good people. I wish we could have stayed longer, sadly my job only pays me if I return to work after vacation! This is not for someone who usually stays at the Hilton, this place is for an adventurer. I'd suggest the adventure though because it is a really fun place to stay. I was glad to see the real Georgia and not some commercialized big box version! </p><span data-reactid="1020">Katherine</span><span data-reactid="1021">2016-04-01T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1022"><p data-reactid="1023">This was a convenient location about 20 minutes outside of Chattanooga. Neal was quick to communicate and return messages. Checking in and out was simple (we checked in late at night, not a problem). Coffee and some granola bars were thoughtfully provided in the room. Since it is only $35, you will be walking across a working garage to get to the bathroom, which is a work-in-progress auto garage bathroom, but the toilet and shower are clean! There are many pets on the property, including the horse that met us at the gate upon arrival, and the many dogs that ushered us out (including one cute little puppy that tried to climb into my car and come home with me). We were just looking for a place to crash, shower, and hit the road again, and this fit the bill. I wish we'd had the chance to check out the property! </p><span data-reactid="1024">Cecily</span><span data-reactid="1025">2015-06-28T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1026"><p data-reactid="1027">Very cool place to stay. The bathroom isn't great, but everything else was perfect. Will definitely come back.</p><span data-reactid="1028">Zach</span><span data-reactid="1029">2016-04-17T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1030"><p data-reactid="1031">Amy and friends were so nice! We were checking out Chattanooga on our way North for thanksgiving. She had great tips for things to see and do. Later that evening they treated us to a bon fire and bbq. Our kids had a blast playing with Neal's. We would definitely go back!</p><span data-reactid="1032">Jimmy</span><span data-reactid="1033">2015-11-23T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1034"><p data-reactid="1035">Neal and Amy were great hosts! Neal responded very quickly to my reservation request and we were given a tour of the property as soon as we got there. If you are a high maintenance traveler or very particular about your accommodations, this place is not for you. If you travel on a tight budget and like a little adventure in your life, then yes, absolutely stay here. I'll stay here next time I'm in the Chattanooga area. Thanks Neal and Amy for being very welcoming. </p><span data-reactid="1036">Josh</span><span data-reactid="1037">2015-07-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1038"><p data-reactid="1039">We had a great time visiting Amy! The room was super cool and the host was even better. I would highly recommend staying here, especially if you are looking for a unique place.</p><span data-reactid="1040">Luke</span><span data-reactid="1041">2015-08-03T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1042"><p data-reactid="1043">If you’re looking for a cheap place to stay for a night or two with a nice ‘horror’ movie feel to it, then this is the place for you! When you pull up to this expanse of land housing an old school house, auto shop, a horse, injured dogs, and a plethora of unique individuals, you will feel perfectly safe surrounded by a barbed wire fence with a single gate to get in and out, which doubles as a way to keep the horse, or anything else, inside. You will most likely be greeted by a pack of limping dogs as well as any number of residents. When you go into the auto shop you are welcomed by a ‘do not enter’ sign and walk into a refreshing garage, perfect for those hot days, there are enough tools around the shop to be used as toys, weapons, or killing any eight legged pests you may come across. The auto shop rooms are as described, there is one queen size bed as well as a large couch and two loft beds. The couch I’m assuming is a new design that was created so that every time you sit down on it a dust-like powder rises from the couch, adding to the ambiance of the room. The bathroom is made easy to use since there is no heavy door in the way that you have to pry open and close to get to the room with the shower. On the property you can relax by the tranquil bathtub of koi fish, or hang out in the kitchen and use its single box of spices, although if you use the kitchen appliances the pots and pans on their own will most likely add flavor to the food. While exploring the area you may be lucky enough to find a noose, several burn piles, and maybe even ‘stubs’ the friendly cat with no tail. The roof is even available to climb onto, there is a ladder leaning against the building, to find it look for the handy grave marker, the roof provides a great view of the property! When back in your room there is even a nifty way to know when it is time to pack up and leave! When the single light goes out and won’t turn back on, you know the time has come, but don’t worry it will turn back on as you start packing up your car! It’s just the property’s way of telling you when it is time to go! Unfortunately we only got to stay for 2 hours until the light decided it was our time to go, but I would definitely recommend the auto shop at Amy’s if you are looking for a stay with a special ‘ominous’ feel. </p><span data-reactid="1044">sydney</span><span data-reactid="1045">2016-03-11T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                         <li data-reactid="1046"><p data-reactid="1047">We enjoyed our stay with Amy! Definitely read through the reviews if you've never stayed here before. The place is just like the description and how several other reviews describe it. Think of it like camping with shelter, however the bedroom was nicer than expected. Very cozy bed and there's a lamp in the other room you can use if you're not a fan of fluorescent lighting. The bathroom/shower is on the other side of the auto shop garage and it's connected to a permanent resident's room however, you can lock the bathroom and shower area while you're in there. If you're only in town for a couple of days and would rather spend money on cool things to do during the day/night and just need a place to crash (would rather save money on lodging), it's a decent place for sure. The dogs were sweet (we also didn't bring any other pets with us.) Location is great because it's pretty close to a lot of cool nature areas while not being too far from downtown Chattanooga. Amy was very hospitable and gave us a tour of the place upon arrival and was there if we ever needed anything. Interesting history of the schoolhouse! They could def make a business in doing a haunted house/haunted prom theme for Halloween if they wanted to. The bathroom in the school apparently didn't flush and some plumbing was being fixed, but we weren't staying in that part so it was fine. If you're adventurous and would like a cheap, unique, interesting/quirky place to crash for a few days, def check this place out! </p><span data-reactid="1048">Morgan</span><span data-reactid="1049">2016-04-06T00:00:00Z</span></li>
